<h2 class="kt-adv-heading2299_eb7911-3f wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading2299_eb7911-3f"><strong><strong>Welcome to Doggone Baking</strong></strong></h2>
</div></div>

</div></div></div></div>



<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column2299_b17276-39"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<h4 class="kt-adv-heading2299_94f9e5-a2 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading2299_94f9e5-a2">Hi, I’m Jennifer Sterbenz, the baker, researcher, and pie fanatic behind Doggone Baking. I developed a passion for baking while studying biology in college. After graduating, I worked as a research assistant until 2018, when I decided to trade lab coats for flour-dusted aprons and moved to California to pursue baking full-time.</h4>

<a href="https://doggonebaking.com/2025/09/15/oreo-pie-crust-recipe/" class="kb-advanced-heading-link kt-adv-heading-link2299_da6770-93"><h2 class="kt-adv-heading2299_da6770-93 wp-block-kadence-advancedheading" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading2299_da6770-93">Oreo Cookie Pie Crust</h2></a>
